# <a name="responsecode"></a><span data-ttu-id="c7554-103">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7554-103">ResponseCode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c7554-104">Das **Response Code** -Element stellt Statusinformationen zur Anforderung bereit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7554-104">The **ResponseCode** element provides status information about the request.</span></span> 
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="c7554-105">ResponseMessage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7554-105">ResponseMessage</span></span>](responsemessage.md) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="c7554-106">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7554-106">ResponseCode</span></span>](responsecode.md)
  
```XML
<ResponseCode/>
```

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="c7554-1479">Bemerkungen</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7554-1479">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c7554-1480">Dieses Element ist nicht erforderlich und wird nicht in allen Antworten berücksichtigt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7554-1480">This element is not required and is not included in all responses.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="c7554-1481">Das Schema, das dieses Element beschreibt, befindet sich im virtuellen IIS-Verzeichnis, das Exchange-Webdienste hostet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7554-1481">The schema that describes this element is located in the IIS virtual directory that hosts Exchange Web Services.</span></span>
